### 40.1  Relationship to Volume 1
Volume 1 (Companion v1.0, sections 00-39) gave one reference of each kind: one full crawler adapter (ARMP), one full pattern (P-A-001), one full worker (worker-pattern), the LLM tier router, the Bayesian engine, two frontend pages, the prompt library, and the phase-by-phase Claude Code prompts. The intent was that the agent would extrapolate from each reference to its siblings.
Volume 2 removes the extrapolation requirement. Every remaining adapter, pattern, worker, contract, host service, config, frontend page, fixture, and helper is given here in full. The two volumes together with SRD v3.0 are the complete build pack.

### 40.2  Structure

### 40.3  Code in this volume is REFERENCE, not GOSPEL
Selectors, schemas, and file structures here reflect the architect's best understanding as of April 2026. Live ministry websites change. International sanctions feeds reformat. Prior calibrations drift. Treat the code as the agent's starting point, not its frozen output.
First-contact protocol applies to every adapter. On first run, an adapter that fails to parse rows must save the live HTML to /infra/sites/<id>.html and notify the architect, NOT silently update its own selectors.
Pattern priors are seeds. Prior values come from the SRD's expected_hit_rate plus initial calibration; they are revised quarterly via the pillar-rotated proposal mechanism (SRD §23).
Solidity addresses in this volume are placeholders. Real deployments produce addresses recorded at /infra/contracts/deployments/{network}.json.

### 40.4  Numbering convention
Volume 1 ends at §39. Volume 2 begins at §41 (one gap reserved). Subsections within a section follow §X.Y / §X.Y.Z form. Code listings have explicit file paths in their heading; the file is to be created at that path verbatim.

### 41.1  packages/adapters/src/minmap-categorisation/index.ts
Source: ministerial procurement categorisations from MINMAP. Lists pre-qualified contractors by category and capability tier. Used to detect debarment-bypass and beneficial-ownership patterns.

### 41.2  packages/adapters/src/coleps/index.ts
Source: COLEPS = Comite de Liquidation et d'Examen des Plaintes et Sinistres. Adjudicates procurement disputes. Output: complaint resolutions, penalty decisions.

### 41.3  packages/adapters/src/minfi/index.ts
Source: MINFI publishes treasury circulars, payment orders for major contracts, debt-to-supplier registers. Lower volume than ARMP but higher signal.

### 41.4  packages/adapters/src/dgb/index.ts
Source: Direction Generale du Budget. Publishes the annual Budget d'Investissement Public (BIP) and quarterly execution reports.

### 41.5  packages/adapters/src/dgtcfm/index.ts
Source: Direction Generale du Tresor, de la Cooperation Financiere et Monetaire. Treasury arrears registers and supplier debt schedules.

### 41.6  packages/adapters/src/minepat/index.ts
Source: Ministere de l'Economie, de la Planification et de l'Amenagement du Territoire. Project pipelines and regional development indicators. Partial JSON API.

### 41.7  packages/adapters/src/rccm/index.ts
Source: Registre du Commerce et du Credit Mobilier. Corporate filings, beneficial-ownership disclosures, director rolls. Cloudflare-protected; uses residential proxy class.

### 41.8  packages/adapters/src/cour-des-comptes/index.ts
Source: Cour des Comptes. Annual and special audit reports. Output: audit_report document captures with paragraph-level extraction triggers.

### 41.9  packages/adapters/src/journal-officiel/index.ts
Source: Journal Officiel de la Republique du Cameroun. Decrees, ministerial orders, debarment publications. Captcha-protected; requires 2Captcha.

### 41.10  packages/adapters/src/anif/index.ts
Source: Agence Nationale d'Investigation Financiere (FIU). Public sanctions, suspicious-transaction summary statistics. Hybrid HTML + JSON feed.

### 42.1  Shared template
Sectoral ministries publish tender notices, awards, and execution reports on similar templates. The six adapters MINTP, MINEE, MINSANTE, MINEDUB, MINESEC, MINHDU share a common structure with parameter substitution. We define the template once and parameterise.

### 45.1  packages/patterns/src/category-a/p-a-002-split-tender.ts
A single procurement need is divided into multiple smaller tenders, each below the public-tender threshold (typically 50M XAF), to evade open competition. Detection: same procuring entity, similar object, awards within a 60-day window summing above the threshold.

### 52.4  Pattern registry


### 53.1  apps/worker-document/src/document.processor.ts
OCR + classify + language detection. Consumes documents from the document_ocr queue. Pulls bytes from the document store by CID, runs Tesseract for scans, runs PDFium text-extract for digital PDFs, runs cld3 for language detection, then a small classifier prompt to assign document_type (tender_notice, award_notice, audit_report, contract, amendment, court_judgement, debarment, ministerial_order, other).

### 53.2  apps/worker-extract/src/extract.processor.ts
Pattern evidence extraction worker. Consumes pattern matches from the pattern_extracted queue, calls patternEvidencePrompt at sonnet tier with structured JSON schema, persists FindingDraft records that worker-bayesian then picks up.

### 53.3  apps/worker-bayesian/src/bayesian.processor.ts
Cross-finding aggregation. Most per-finding posterior is computed inline by worker-pattern (v1 §16). worker-bayesian handles the corroboration ledger across findings, which adjusts posteriors when multiple independent patterns hit the same entity.

### 53.4  apps/worker-counter-evidence/src/counter.processor.ts
Devil's advocate worker. Triggered on findings where posterior crosses 0.85. Calls devilsAdvocatePrompt at sonnet/opus tier, attaches the rebuttal to the finding's audit chain. Per §18.2 anti-hallucination wrapper, the devil's advocate is required to either find rebuttal or explicitly report 'no rebuttal identified, no fabrication.'

### 53.5  apps/worker-dossier/src/dossier.processor.ts
Dossier renderer. Triggered when a finding's posterior crosses 0.85 (escalation_candidate tier). Renders bilingual PDF dossier with cover, summary in FR + EN, evidence ledger, counter-evidence section, methodology appendix, and Polygon anchor reference.

### 53.6  apps/worker-conac-sftp/src/conac-sftp.processor.ts
CONAC delivery flow per SRD §06. Renders dossier package, encrypts with CONAC public key, uploads to CONAC SFTP, polls for ACK file, persists ACK to delivery_log, anchors a delivery_anchored event.

### 53.7  apps/worker-minfi-api/src/minfi-api.module.ts + scoring.controller.ts
Fastify-mounted MINFI scoring service. Receives entity scoring requests on POST /api/v1/score, returns JSON body with risk band, contributing findings, and dossier links.

### 53.8  apps/worker-tip-triage/src/tip.processor.ts
Whistleblower tip triage. Receives tips via the public Tip-In adapter (per SRD §13), calls tipClassifyPrompt, auto-dismisses spam, and promotes signal-bearing tips into pattern-detection candidates.

### 53.9  apps/audit-verifier/src/audit.runner.ts
Nightly audit-verifier (SRD §28). Walks the hash chain, recomputes block hashes, recomputes ECE and Brier on the past quarter, recomputes telemetry health (queue ages, dead-letter counts, drift indicators). Emits a single audit-summary doc anchored with auditChainAdvanced event.

### 59.1  /opt/vigil/services/polygon-signer/server.ts

### 59.2  /opt/vigil/services/polygon-signer/yubikey-bridge.js
YubiKey 9c bridge. Uses node-pcsc plus a small ASN.1 ECDSA serializer. The PIV slot must be 9c; loaded with a secp256k1 key generated during the signing ceremony. The Vault scope token proves authorisation; the device PIN is read from Vault transit (never written to disk).

### 59.3  /etc/systemd/system/vigil-signer.service

### 60.1  /etc/systemd/system/vigil-vault-unseal.service

### 60.2  /etc/systemd/system/vigil-watchdog.service + /opt/vigil/scripts/watchdog.ts
Health monitor. Runs every 60s, verifies that workers' BullMQ heartbeats are within 90s, that Postgres queries respond < 500ms, that the Polygon signer socket accepts connections, and that the dead-letter queue is below threshold. On failure, posts to the architect's wire-channel via the watchdog webhook.

### 61.1  Topology
HashiCorp Vault is the secrets backbone for the entire platform. Every credential -- adapter site logins, IRC database password, OpenSearch token, MinIO root key, Polygon RPC URL, the secp256k1 anchor key on the YubiKey -- is fetched at boot time from Vault, never written to disk in plaintext. Vault is sealed at startup and unsealed by the architect's 3-of-5 Shamir shares (separate from the 3-of-5 council key).
Five role policies cover the full system. Each is mounted at a fixed path under sys/policy/:

### 61.2  policies/architect.hcl

### 61.3  policies/dashboard.hcl

### 61.4  policies/worker.hcl

### 61.5  policies/polygon-signer.hcl

### 61.6  policies/tip-handler.hcl

### 61.7  Bootstrap script


### 62.1  Realm topology
Keycloak is the single OIDC issuer for the platform. One realm: 'vigil'. Two clients: 'vigil-dashboard' (Next.js SPA + SSR) and 'vigil-api' (Fastify API + worker callbacks). Six roles cover the full operator/council/audit/public matrix.

### 62.2  realm-export.json (excerpt - WebAuthn flow)


### 62.3  Sample user creation (council member)


### 63.1  Hardening intent
Caddy is the public-facing edge. It terminates TLS via Let's Encrypt automation, rate-limits the public tip endpoint and verify endpoint, and forwards everything else to the dashboard, API, or Keycloak as appropriate. The Caddyfile in this section is the production version; staging swaps the hostnames and uses Let's Encrypt staging.

### 63.2  packages/host-config/caddy/Caddyfile



### 64.1  Image strategy
Three base layers reduce duplication and rebuild surface across the fleet:
vigil-base-node: Debian slim + Node 20 LTS + tini + non-root user vigil:1001 + locale C.UTF-8
vigil-base-worker: extends vigil-base-node + pnpm 9.7 + the @vigil/* shared workspace + healthcheck script
vigil-base-adapter: extends vigil-base-worker + Playwright + Chromium + poppler-utils + tor + clamav + ClamAV virus DB

### 64.10  Per-worker Dockerfile reference table
Each worker has its own Dockerfile in apps/worker-<name>/Dockerfile that follows the §64.7 template. The only difference between worker Dockerfiles is the WORKER_NAME ARG and the COPY paths to that worker's specific package.



### 65.1  Migration strategy
Drizzle ORM with PostgreSQL 16. Migrations are versioned files in packages/db/migrations/, generated by `pnpm db:generate` and applied by `pnpm db:migrate`. The architect runs migrations manually via the dashboard's /admin/migrations panel; never auto-applied by worker boot. Each migration is signed into the audit chain at the moment of application.

### 67.1  Why synthesise
Real ARMP award notices, RCCM extracts, decrees, etc. are copyrighted and partly sensitive. The synthetic-findings pipeline needs PDFs that LOOK like real ones (same layout, same fields, same fonts) but contain made-up data. The mock generator produces these.
This is also a useful CI artefact: when an adapter test runs in CI, the generator produces a brand-new PDF with a fresh hash, exercising the artefact-hash path end-to-end without committing PDFs to git.

### 67.2  scripts/generate-mock-documents.ts


### 68.1  Initial 50, target 200
Volume 1 ships with 50 entries seeded by the architect during Phase 9. Beyond 50, ECE per pattern category becomes meaningful only with sample sizes of 30+ per bin per category. Reaching ~200 entries within 6 months is the realistic target. The growth protocol below is the discipline.

### 68.2  Calibration entry schema

### 68.3  Growth protocol (architect responsibility)
Every Friday: walk all findings closed in the previous week with `closure_reason IN ('confirmed', 'dismissed_evidence_insufficient', 'dismissed_counter_evidence', 'council_rejected', 'investigation_completed')`
For each: record a calibration entry with the posterior at time of review and the ground_truth label justified by at least one cited piece of evidence
Compute ECE per pattern category every Sunday night (worker job). If any category breaches 0.10, raise an alert; the architect retraces priors that week
After 6 months: review every entry older than 90 days. If new evidence has surfaced (e.g. a court judgement), update the ground_truth and re-record
The calibration set is itself anchored: the calibration_run audit event commits a Merkle root of all entries at that snapshot

### 68.4  scripts/seed-calibration.ts

### 68.5  scripts/compute-ece.ts (weekly cron)



### 69.1  Why a forensics package
Several patterns rely on signals the LLM cannot extract reliably from raw text. Pattern P-G-001 (backdating) needs file-modification metadata that survives PDF cleaners. Pattern P-G-002 (signature mismatch) needs a perceptual-hash comparison between two signature image regions. Pattern P-G-003 (font tampering) needs a font-embedding diff. These signals belong in deterministic helpers that can be called by the worker-pattern dispatcher.

### 70.1  Use cases
Pattern category D needs satellite imagery as ground-truth corroboration. The most common cases:
P-D-001: contract claims 'roadworks complete' at coordinates X,Y with date Z; satellite image at Z+30d shows no construction trace
P-D-002: contract claims 'building rehabilitated'; before/after image diff shows unchanged structure
P-D-003: contract location coordinates are inconsistent with claimed administrative region

### 70.2  packages/satellite-client/src/index.ts

### 70.3  packages/satellite-client/src/types.ts

### 70.4  packages/satellite-client/src/sentinel-hub.ts

### 70.5  packages/satellite-client/src/change-detection.ts



### 71.1  When to reach for graph
Patterns in category F (related-party signals) and B (corporate-form signals) need graph traversal: shared directors, shared addresses, round-trip ownership. PostgreSQL handles two-hop joins acceptably; beyond that, Neo4j with Cypher is dramatically faster and more readable. The graph store is read-only from the worker side; it is rebuilt nightly from PostgreSQL by an ETL job.

### 71.2  packages/graph-queries/src/index.ts

### 72.1  What is now in the build pack
Three documents loaded together cover ~90-95% of the work that, six months ago, would have required either an architect-led artisanal build or a full external integrator. The remaining 5-10% is institutional, political, and physical: things no document can do for the architect.

### 72.2  Detailed completion ledger

### 72.3  What remains forever-architect-only
Some work cannot be in any document. These are the irreducible things the architect does in person. The agent can prepare the ground, but cannot stand in:
Hardware procurement and provisioning of YubiKeys (5 council kits + 1 architect kit + 2 spares + 1 polygon signer kit). Source from a reseller in person; verify firmware signatures upon receipt; do not buy online.
BIOS/firmware setup of host servers: TPM enrolment, Secure Boot keys, IPMI password rotation, network bootstrap. Done at the rack, not over SSH.
CONAC institutional credentials: the architect must obtain the official engagement letter, the SFTP delivery account, the dossier-format approval. No agent can negotiate this.
Council member identity verification: matching pillar-holder names to physical persons. The architect signs off in person; the agent only stores their public keys after verification.
Council politics: alignment between executive secretary expectations, council composition, recusal rules per case. Documents codify the process, but each finding's first escalation requires architect judgement on tone and timing.
First-contact protocol for each adapter: the manual fetches that probe live ministry websites, the conversation with the relevant agency's communications officer if you decide to disclose, the reading of robots.txt and ToS in the context of public-interest journalism precedent in Cameroonian law.
Calibration ground truth labelling: the first 50 entries cannot be auto-graded. The architect labels them after walking through real findings against real outcomes. Subsequent entries can be labelled by senior operators, but the first batch is the architect's discipline.
Crisis decisions: when an adversary attacks the system or attempts to compromise a council member, the response is human. The agent logs and assists; it does not decide.
Public communications: when a finding becomes public (justice, journalism, parliamentary inquiry), the framing is the architect's. The system does not speak for itself in the press.
Periodic dignity and burnout checks: VIGIL APEX is high-stakes anti-corruption work in a hostile environment. The architect's stamina is itself a critical infrastructure resource. No document can preserve it; only honest self-assessment and a defined exit protocol can.

### 72.4  How to use this volume during the build
The two volumes work in concert. During each phase:
Volume 1 §28-37 contains the prompt that initiates that phase with the agent.
Volume 1's reference implementations show the agent the canonical pattern for that phase's artefact (one of each kind).
Volume 2's section for that artefact category shows the agent the remaining instances (the other 25 adapters, the other 42 patterns, etc.).
Volume 1's prompt library (§18-26) is loaded into the agent's context as the runtime LLM-orchestration system.
The SRD is the binding spec for acceptance: each phase's exit criteria are checked against SRD wording.

### 72.5  Brittleness, honestly
This volume contains thousands of lines of TypeScript and Solidity that have not yet met their target environments. Several will need rework on day-one of contact:
Adapter selectors: every regulator's website has its own DOM idiosyncrasies. The selectors in Part G are derived from publicly visible structures, but no architect should expect them to be intact next month. The first-contact protocol in v1 §06 is the regeneration mechanism.
Pattern priors: the BASE_RATE=0.05 and per-pattern multipliers in Part H are seeded from the architect's prior reading of Cameroonian procurement literature. Phase 9 calibration will adjust them; expect the priors to move 10-30% in either direction within the first 6 months.
Smart contract parameters: the gas limits, dispute window, quorum threshold in §58 are sensible defaults but assume Polygon mainnet conditions stable as of model knowledge cutoff. Verify gas price fundamentals on the day of deployment.
Caddy rate limits and Docker resource constraints: tuned conservatively. Real traffic patterns from Phase 9 will provide the data to relax or tighten.
Forensics thresholds (PHASH_RATIO_THRESHOLD, font_introduction_year, NDVI delta cutoffs): chosen to be cautious. Tune against the architect's own document collection during the build.

### 72.6  Closing
VIGIL APEX is now buildable. The architect, working with Claude Code and these three documents, can produce the running system in 8-14 weeks of dedicated effort. The remaining variability is the institutional and human work, not the technical work. The work the architect cannot delegate is the work that matters most: the first calibration pass, the first council sign-off, the first dossier landing on the desk of a serious investigator, the first time the system identifies a finding that, in retrospect, mattered.
The system was always going to take judgement to operate. These documents reduce the technical-decision burden enough that the architect's judgement can be reserved for the questions only judgement can answer. That's the design intent. That's the deliverable.

END OF VOLUME 2

For Junior Thuram Nana, Sovereign Architect

| import { chromium } from 'playwright'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef, AdapterRunContext, AdapterResult } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup'; import { fetchAndPin } from '../../lib/document'; import { sleep } from '../../lib/time';   const BASE = 'https://minmap.cm';   const CategorisationRowSchema = z.object({   ref:               z.string().min(3),   contractor:        z.string(),   rccm:              z.string().nullable(),   category:          z.enum(['BTP','TPB','EQUIPEMENTS','SERVICES','FOURNITURES','CONSEIL','MIXTE']),   capability_tier:   z.enum(['T1','T2','T3','T4','T5']),   granted_at:        z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   expires_at:        z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   decision_url:      z.string().url().optional() });   export const minmapCategorisationAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'minmap-categorisation',   source: 'Ministere des Marches Publics - Categorisations',   baseUrl: BASE,   schedule: '0 3 * * *',   proxyClass: 'datacenter',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.4, burst: 2 },   failureBudget: 5,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage, signal } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? ''));             if (cells.length < 7) continue;               const parsed = CategorisationRowSchema.parse({               ref:             cells[0],               contractor:      cells[1],               rccm:            cells[2] \|\| null,               category:        cells[3],               capability_tier: cells[4],               granted_at:      cells[5],               expires_at:      cells[6],               decision_url:    await r.$eval('a.decision', (a: HTMLAnchorElement) => a.href).catch(() => undefined)             });               if (parsed.granted_at < since) continue;             anyFresh = true;               let docCid: string \| undefined;             if (parsed.decision_url) {               const pin = await fetchAndPin(parsed.decision_url, ctx);               docCid = pin.cid;             }               const dk = dedupKey('minmap.categorisation', parsed.ref, parsed.granted_at.toISOString().slice(0, 10));             if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;               events.push({               kind: 'document.captured',               payload: {                 source: 'minmap-categorisation',                 ref: parsed.ref,                 contractor: parsed.contractor,                 rccm: parsed.rccm,                 category: parsed.category,                 capability_tier: parsed.capability_tier,                 granted_at: parsed.granted_at,                 expires_at: parsed.expires_at,                 documentCid: docCid,                 dedupKey: dk,                 runId: ctx.runId               }             });             emitted++;           } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'minmap.row.parse-failed'); }         }         if (!anyFresh) break;         pageNum++;         if (pageNum > 100) break;       }     } finally {       await browser.close();     }       return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

| import { fetch } from 'undici'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup';   const API = 'https://api.minepat.gov.cm/v1';   const ProjectSchema = z.object({   code:             z.string(),   label:            z.string(),   ministry:         z.string(),   region:           z.string(),   sector:           z.string(),   estimated_xaf:    z.number().nonnegative(),   status:           z.enum(['PLANNED','APPROVED','PROCURING','UNDER_EXECUTION','COMPLETED','SUSPENDED','CANCELLED']),   start_year:       z.number().int(),   end_year:         z.number().int().nullable(),   beneficiary_pop:  z.number().int().nullable(),   last_updated_at:  z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)) });   export const minepatAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'minepat',   source: 'MINEPAT - Pipeline de projets publics',   baseUrl: API,   schedule: '0 8 * * 1',   proxyClass: 'datacenter',   rateLimit: { rps: 1.0, burst: 5 },   failureBudget: 3,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400_000);     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;       let cursor: string \| null = null;     do {       const url = `${API}/projects?since=${since.toISOString()}${cursor ? '&cursor=' + cursor : ''}`;       const res = await fetch(url, {         dispatcher: proxy.toUndici(),         headers: { 'accept': 'application/json', 'user-agent': 'VIGIL-APEX/1.0' }       });       fetched++;       if (!res.ok) {         errors++;         logger.warn({ status: res.status, url }, 'minepat.api.error');         break;       }       const body = await res.json() as { items: unknown[]; next_cursor: string \| null };       for (const item of body.items) {         try {           const parsed = ProjectSchema.parse(item);           const dk = dedupKey('minepat.project', parsed.code, parsed.last_updated_at.toISOString().slice(0, 10));           if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;           events.push({             kind: 'document.captured',             payload: {               source: 'minepat',               project_code: parsed.code,               project_label: parsed.label,               ministry: parsed.ministry,               region: parsed.region,               sector: parsed.sector,               estimated_xaf: parsed.estimated_xaf,               status: parsed.status,               start_year: parsed.start_year,               end_year: parsed.end_year,               beneficiary_pop: parsed.beneficiary_pop,               last_updated_at: parsed.last_updated_at,               dedupKey: dk,               runId: ctx.runId             }           });           emitted++;         } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'minepat.item.parse-failed'); }       }       cursor = body.next_cursor;     } while (cursor);       return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

### Table 9

| import { chromium } from 'playwright'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup'; import { fetchAndPin } from '../../lib/document'; import { sleep } from '../../lib/time';   const BASE = 'https://rccm.cm';   const FilingRowSchema = z.object({   rccm_number:       z.string(),   filing_type:       z.enum(['INCORPORATION','AMENDMENT','DIRECTOR_CHANGE','UBO_DISCLOSURE','LIQUIDATION','OTHER']),   entity_name:       z.string(),   legal_form:        z.string().nullable(),   capital_xaf:       z.number().nonnegative().nullable(),   filed_at:          z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   directors:         z.array(z.string()).max(20).default([]),   ubos:              z.array(z.object({ name: z.string(), pct: z.number().min(0).max(100) })).default([]),   document_url:      z.string().url().optional() });   export const rccmAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'rccm',   source: 'Registre du Commerce et du Credit Mobilier',   baseUrl: BASE,   schedule: '0 9 * * *',   proxyClass: 'residential',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.2, burst: 1 },   failureBudget: 4,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage, signal } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? ''));             if (cells.length < 6) continue;             const directors = await r.$$eval('ul.directors li', (lis) => lis.map((li) => li.textContent?.trim() ?? ''));             const parsed = FilingRowSchema.parse({               rccm_number:    cells[0],               filing_type:    cells[1],               entity_name:    cells[2],               legal_form:     cells[3] \|\| null,               capital_xaf:    cells[4] ? Number(cells[4].replace(/[^0-9]/g, '')) : null,               filed_at:       cells[5],               directors:      directors,               ubos:           [],               document_url:   await r.$eval('a.detail', (a: HTMLAnchorElement) => a.href).catch(() => undefined)             });             if (parsed.filed_at < since) continue;             anyFresh = true;             const docCid = parsed.document_url ? (await fetchAndPin(parsed.document_url, ctx)).cid : undefined;             const dk = dedupKey('rccm.filing', parsed.rccm_number, parsed.filed_at.toISOString().slice(0, 10), parsed.filing_type);             if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;             events.push({               kind: 'document.captured',               payload: {                 source: 'rccm',                 rccm_number: parsed.rccm_number,                 filing_type: parsed.filing_type,                 entity_name: parsed.entity_name,                 legal_form: parsed.legal_form,                 capital_xaf: parsed.capital_xaf,                 filed_at: parsed.filed_at,                 directors: parsed.directors,                 ubos: parsed.ubos,                 documentCid: docCid,                 dedupKey: dk,                 runId: ctx.runId               }             });             emitted++;           } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'rccm.row.parse-failed'); }         }         if (!anyFresh) break;         pageNum++;         if (pageNum > 100) break;       }     } finally { await browser.close(); }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

| import { chromium } from 'playwright'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup'; import { fetchAndPin } from '../../lib/document'; import { sleep } from '../../lib/time';   const BASE = 'https://courdescomptes.cm';   const AuditReportSchema = z.object({   ref:           z.string(),   title:         z.string(),   audited_entity: z.string(),   fiscal_period: z.string(),   published_at:  z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   report_url:    z.string().url(),   summary_url:   z.string().url().optional() });   export const courDesComptesAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'cour-des-comptes',   source: 'Cour des Comptes - Rapports d\'Audit',   baseUrl: BASE,   schedule: '0 10 * * 1,4',   proxyClass: 'datacenter',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.3, burst: 1 },   failureBudget: 4,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage, signal } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 86400_000);     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;     const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true, proxy: proxy.toPlaywright() });     try {       const page = await (await browser.newContext({ locale: 'fr-FR' })).newPage();       let pageNum = 1;       while (!signal.aborted) {         await page.goto(`${BASE}/rapports?page=${pageNum}`, { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });         fetched++;         await sleep(2500);         const cards = await page.$$('article.report-card');         if (cards.length === 0) break;         let anyFresh = false;         for (const c of cards) {           try {             const ref = await c.$eval('.ref', (el) => el.textContent?.trim() ?? '');             const title = await c.$eval('h3.title', (el) => el.textContent?.trim() ?? '');             const entity = await c.$eval('.entity', (el) => el.textContent?.trim() ?? '');             const period = await c.$eval('.period', (el) => el.textContent?.trim() ?? '');             const publishedAt = await c.$eval('time', (el) => el.getAttribute('datetime') ?? '');             const reportUrl = await c.$eval('a.download-pdf', (a: HTMLAnchorElement) => a.href);             const parsed = AuditReportSchema.parse({               ref, title, audited_entity: entity, fiscal_period: period,               published_at: publishedAt, report_url: reportUrl             });             if (parsed.published_at < since) continue;             anyFresh = true;             const docCid = (await fetchAndPin(parsed.report_url, ctx)).cid;             const dk = dedupKey('cour-comptes.report', parsed.ref);             if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;             events.push({               kind: 'document.captured',               payload: {                 source: 'cour-des-comptes',                 ref: parsed.ref,                 title: parsed.title,                 audited_entity: parsed.audited_entity,                 fiscal_period: parsed.fiscal_period,                 published_at: parsed.published_at,                 document_type: 'audit_report',                 documentCid: docCid,                 dedupKey: dk,                 runId: ctx.runId               }             });             emitted++;           } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'cour-comptes.card.parse-failed'); }         }         if (!anyFresh) break;         pageNum++;         if (pageNum > 30) break;       }     } finally { await browser.close(); }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

### Table 11

| import { chromium } from 'playwright'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup'; import { fetchAndPin } from '../../lib/document'; import { solveTwoCaptcha } from '../../lib/captcha'; import { sleep } from '../../lib/time';   const BASE = 'https://journalofficiel.cm';   const PublicationSchema = z.object({   ref:            z.string(),   publication_no: z.string(),   type:           z.enum(['DECREE','MINISTERIAL_ORDER','DEBARMENT','APPOINTMENT','LAW','REGULATION','OTHER']),   title:          z.string(),   published_at:   z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   signing_authority: z.string().nullable(),   full_text_url:  z.string().url() });   export const journalOfficielAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'journal-officiel',   source: 'Journal Officiel de la Republique du Cameroun',   baseUrl: BASE,   schedule: '0 11 * * *',   proxyClass: 'residential',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.15, burst: 1 },   failureBudget: 5,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage, signal } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? new Date(Date.now() - 14 * 86400_000);     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;       const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true, proxy: proxy.toPlaywright() });     try {       const page = await (await browser.newContext({ locale: 'fr-FR' })).newPage();       await page.goto(`${BASE}/recherche`, { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });       fetched++;       // Captcha gate       const captchaImg = await page.$('img.captcha').catch(() => null);       if (captchaImg) {         const captchaSrc = await captchaImg.getAttribute('src');         const solution = await solveTwoCaptcha(captchaSrc!);         await page.fill('input[name=captcha]', solution);       }       await page.fill('input[name=date_from]', since.toISOString().slice(0, 10));       await page.click('button[type=submit]');       await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');       await sleep(3000);         let pageNum = 1;       while (!signal.aborted) {         const rows = await page.$$('table.publications tbody tr');         if (rows.length === 0) break;         for (const r of rows) {           try {             const cells = await r.$$eval('td', (tds) => tds.map((td) => td.textContent?.trim() ?? ''));             if (cells.length < 6) continue;             const parsed = PublicationSchema.parse({               ref:               cells[0],               publication_no:    cells[1],               type:              cells[2],               title:             cells[3],               published_at:      cells[4],               signing_authority: cells[5] \|\| null,               full_text_url:     await r.$eval('a.pdf', (a: HTMLAnchorElement) => a.href)             });             const docCid = (await fetchAndPin(parsed.full_text_url, ctx)).cid;             const dk = dedupKey('journal-officiel.publication', parsed.ref, parsed.publication_no);             if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;             events.push({               kind: parsed.type === 'DEBARMENT' ? 'debarment.issued' : 'document.captured',               payload: {                 source: 'journal-officiel',                 ref: parsed.ref,                 publication_no: parsed.publication_no,                 type: parsed.type,                 title: parsed.title,                 published_at: parsed.published_at,                 signing_authority: parsed.signing_authority,                 documentCid: docCid,                 dedupKey: dk,                 runId: ctx.runId               }             });             emitted++;           } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'journal-off.row.parse-failed'); }         }         const next = await page.$('a.pagination-next:not(.disabled)').catch(() => null);         if (!next) break;         await next.click();         await page.waitForLoadState('networkidle');         await sleep(3000);         pageNum++;         if (pageNum > 30) break;       }     } finally { await browser.close(); }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

| import { fetch } from 'undici'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup';   const API = 'https://anif.cm/api/v1';   const SanctionSchema = z.object({   ref:           z.string(),   party_name:    z.string(),   party_type:    z.enum(['INDIVIDUAL','ENTITY']),   sanction_type: z.enum(['ASSET_FREEZE','TRAVEL_BAN','SUSPENSION','LICENSE_REVOCATION','PUBLIC_WARNING']),   effective_at:  z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   expires_at:    z.string().nullable().transform((s) => s ? new Date(s) : null),   rationale:     z.string(),   document_url:  z.string().url().optional() });   export const anifAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'anif',   source: 'ANIF - Sanctions Publiques',   baseUrl: API,   schedule: '0 12 * * *',   proxyClass: 'datacenter',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.5, burst: 2 },   failureBudget: 4,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage } = ctx;     const since = ctx.since ?? new Date(Date.now() - 30 * 86400_000);     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;       const res = await fetch(`${API}/sanctions?since=${since.toISOString()}`, {       dispatcher: proxy.toUndici(),       headers: { 'accept': 'application/json' }     });     fetched++;     if (!res.ok) {       logger.error({ status: res.status }, 'anif.api.error');       return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors: 1 } };     }     const body = await res.json() as { items: unknown[] };     for (const item of body.items) {       try {         const parsed = SanctionSchema.parse(item);         const dk = dedupKey('anif.sanction', parsed.ref, parsed.effective_at.toISOString().slice(0, 10));         if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;         events.push({           kind: 'debarment.issued',           payload: {             source: 'anif',             ref: parsed.ref,             party_name: parsed.party_name,             party_type: parsed.party_type,             sanction_type: parsed.sanction_type,             effective_at: parsed.effective_at,             expires_at: parsed.expires_at,             rationale: parsed.rationale,             dedupKey: dk,             runId: ctx.runId           }         });         emitted++;       } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'anif.item.parse-failed'); }     }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

### Table 14

| // packages/adapters/src/lib/sectoral-template.ts import { chromium } from 'playwright'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef, AdapterRunContext, AdapterResult } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from './dedup'; import { fetchAndPin } from './document'; import { sleep } from './time';   export interface SectoralAdapterConfig {   id: string;   source: string;   baseUrl: string;   schedule: string;   tendersPath: string;       // e.g., '/marches'   awardsPath: string;        // e.g., '/attributions'   rowSchema: z.ZodSchema<any>; }   export function makeSectoralAdapter(cfg: SectoralAdapterConfig): AdapterDef {   return {     id: cfg.id,     source: cfg.source,     baseUrl: cfg.baseUrl,     schedule: cfg.schedule,     proxyClass: 'datacenter',     rateLimit: { rps: 0.4, burst: 2 },     failureBudget: 4,       async run(ctx: AdapterRunContext): Promise<AdapterResult> {       const { logger, proxy, storage, signal } = ctx;       const since = ctx.since ?? new Date(Date.now() - 7 * 86400_000);       const events: AdapterResult['events'] = [];       let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;         const browser = await chromium.launch({ headless: true, proxy: proxy.toPlaywright() });       try {         const page = await (await browser.newContext({ locale: 'fr-FR' })).newPage();         for (const path of [cfg.tendersPath, cfg.awardsPath]) {           let pageNum = 1;           while (!signal.aborted) {             await page.goto(`${cfg.baseUrl}${path}?page=${pageNum}`, { waitUntil: 'networkidle' });             fetched++;             await sleep(2000);             const rows = await page.$$('table tbody tr');             if (rows.length === 0) break;             let anyFresh = false;             for (const r of rows) {               try {                 const cells = await r.$$eval('td', (tds) => tds.map((td) => td.textContent?.trim() ?? ''));                 const docHref = await r.$eval('a.detail', (a: HTMLAnchorElement) => a.href).catch(() => undefined);                 const parsed = cfg.rowSchema.parse({ cells, docHref });                 const evtDate = parsed.published_at ?? parsed.award_date;                 if (evtDate < since) continue;                 anyFresh = true;                 const docCid = parsed.document_url ? (await fetchAndPin(parsed.document_url, ctx)).cid : undefined;                 const dk = dedupKey(`${cfg.id}.${path === cfg.tendersPath ? 'tender' : 'award'}`, parsed.ref, evtDate.toISOString().slice(0, 10));                 if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;                 events.push({                   kind: path === cfg.tendersPath ? 'tender.published' : 'award.issued',                   payload: { source: cfg.id, ...parsed, documentCid: docCid, dedupKey: dk, runId: ctx.runId }                 });                 emitted++;               } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e, source: cfg.id }, 'sectoral.row.parse-failed'); }             }             if (!anyFresh) break;             pageNum++;             if (pageNum > 50) break;           }         }       } finally { await browser.close(); }       return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };     }   }; } |

| import { fetch } from 'undici'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup';   const FEED = 'https://www.worldbank.org/en/projects-operations/procurement/debarred-firms.json';   const DebarredFirmSchema = z.object({   firmName:           z.string(),   address:            z.string().nullable(),   country:            z.string(),   ineligibilityFrom:  z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   ineligibilityTo:    z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   groundsForDebarment: z.string() });   export const worldbankSanctionsAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'worldbank-sanctions',   source: 'World Bank - Debarred Firms List',   baseUrl: FEED,   schedule: '0 15 * * 1',   proxyClass: 'tor',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.5, burst: 1 },   failureBudget: 3,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage } = ctx;     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;       const res = await fetch(FEED, { dispatcher: proxy.toUndici() });     fetched++;     if (!res.ok) return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors: 1 } };     const body = await res.json() as { firms: unknown[] };       for (const item of body.firms) {       try {         const parsed = DebarredFirmSchema.parse(item);         // Filter: country == 'Cameroon' OR address contains 'Cameroon'/'Cameroun'         if (parsed.country !== 'Cameroon' && !(parsed.address ?? '').toLowerCase().match(/cameroon\|cameroun/)) continue;         const dk = dedupKey('wb.debarment', parsed.firmName, parsed.ineligibilityFrom.toISOString().slice(0, 10));         if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;         events.push({           kind: 'debarment.issued',           payload: {             source: 'worldbank-sanctions',             party_name: parsed.firmName,             party_type: 'ENTITY',             sanction_type: 'DEBARMENT',             effective_at: parsed.ineligibilityFrom,             expires_at: parsed.ineligibilityTo,             rationale: parsed.groundsForDebarment,             address: parsed.address,             country: parsed.country,             international_body: 'World Bank',             dedupKey: dk,             runId: ctx.runId           }         });         emitted++;       } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'wb.firm.parse-failed'); }     }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

| import { fetch } from 'undici'; import { z } from 'zod'; import type { AdapterDef } from '../contract'; import { dedupKey } from '../../lib/dedup';   const FEED = 'https://www.afdb.org/en/projects-and-operations/procurement/debarment-list/json';   const SchemaA = z.object({   entity_name: z.string(),   type: z.enum(['firm','individual']),   nationality: z.string(),   debarment_start: z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   debarment_end: z.string().transform((s) => new Date(s)),   grounds: z.string() });   export const afdbSanctionsAdapter: AdapterDef = {   id: 'afdb-sanctions',   source: 'African Development Bank - Debarred Entities',   baseUrl: FEED,   schedule: '0 15 * * 1',   proxyClass: 'tor',   rateLimit: { rps: 0.5, burst: 1 },   failureBudget: 3,     async run(ctx) {     const { logger, proxy, storage } = ctx;     const events = [] as any[];     let fetched = 0, emitted = 0, errors = 0;     const res = await fetch(FEED, { dispatcher: proxy.toUndici() });     fetched++;     if (!res.ok) return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors: 1 } };     const body = await res.json() as { entities: unknown[] };     for (const item of body.entities) {       try {         const parsed = SchemaA.parse(item);         if (!parsed.nationality.toLowerCase().match(/cameroon\|cameroun/)) continue;         const dk = dedupKey('afdb.debarment', parsed.entity_name, parsed.debarment_start.toISOString().slice(0, 10));         if (await storage.events.findByDedupKey(dk)) continue;         events.push({           kind: 'debarment.issued',           payload: {             source: 'afdb-sanctions',             party_name: parsed.entity_name,             party_type: parsed.type === 'firm' ? 'ENTITY' : 'INDIVIDUAL',             sanction_type: 'DEBARMENT',             effective_at: parsed.debarment_start,             expires_at: parsed.debarment_end,             rationale: parsed.grounds,             country: parsed.nationality,             international_body: 'AfDB',             dedupKey: dk,             runId: ctx.runId           }         });         emitted++;       } catch (e) { errors++; logger.warn({ err: e }, 'afdb.entity.parse-failed'); }     }     return { events, highWaterMark: ctx.until ?? new Date(), metrics: { fetched, emitted, errors } };   } }; |

| import { z } from 'zod'; import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract';   export const pA002SplitTender: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-A-002',   category: 'A',   display_name_fr: 'Fractionnement de marche',   display_name_en: 'Tender splitting',   severity_baseline: 0.75,   inputs: [{ name: 'tender', source: 'event:tender.published', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.025,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.32,     modifiers: [       { when: 'three_or_more_in_window', delta: +0.15 },       { when: 'same_contractor_across_splits', delta: +0.20 },       { when: 'sum_above_500m_xaf', delta: +0.10 },       { when: 'distinct_subprojects_evidence', delta: -0.20 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const groups = await ctx.db.tenders.findGroupsBySimilarity({       windowDays: 60,       thresholdXaf: 50_000_000,       similarityField: 'object_normalized'     });     for (const g of groups) {       if (g.tenders.length < 2) continue;       const sum = g.tenders.reduce((s, t) => s + t.estimated_value, 0);       if (sum < 50_000_000) continue;       const contractors = new Set(g.tenders.map((t) => t.awarded_to).filter(Boolean));       const sameContractor = contractors.size === 1 && g.tenders.every((t) => t.awarded_to);       let strength = 0.65;       if (g.tenders.length >= 3) strength += 0.10;       if (sameContractor) strength += 0.15;       if (sum >= 500_000_000) strength += 0.05;       strength = Math.min(0.95, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-A-002',         tenderRef: g.tenders[0]!.ref,         strength,         evidence: {           procuring_entity: g.procuring_entity,           tender_count: g.tenders.length,           tender_refs: g.tenders.map((t) => t.ref),           summed_value: sum,           same_contractor: sameContractor,           window_days: 60,           object_normalized: g.object_normalized         },         evidenceCids: g.tenders.map((t) => t.documentCid).filter(Boolean) as string[],         modifiers: {           three_or_more_in_window: g.tenders.length >= 3,           same_contractor_across_splits: sameContractor,           sum_above_500m_xaf: sum >= 500_000_000,           distinct_subprojects_evidence: false         },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

### Table 36

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract';   export const pA003NoBidEmergency: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-A-003',   category: 'A',   display_name_fr: 'Marche d\'urgence sans appel d\'offres',   display_name_en: 'No-bid emergency procurement',   severity_baseline: 0.65,   inputs: [{ name: 'tender', source: 'event:tender.published', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.06,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.22,     modifiers: [       { when: 'amount_above_200m_xaf', delta: +0.12 },       { when: 'predictable_event', delta: +0.18 },       { when: 'genuine_disaster_proximity', delta: -0.20 },       { when: 'recurring_emergency_same_entity', delta: +0.15 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const tenders = await ctx.db.tenders.findRecent({       since: ctx.window.since,       method: 'EMERGENCY'     });     for (const t of tenders) {       const award = await ctx.db.awards.findByTenderRef(t.ref);       if (!award) continue;       const recurringCount = await ctx.db.tenders.countByEntityAndMethod({         entity: t.procuring_entity,         method: 'EMERGENCY',         windowDays: 365       });       const isHighValue = t.estimated_value >= 200_000_000;       const isRecurring = recurringCount >= 5;       // Predictable: schools every September, drought every dry season, etc.       const month = (t.published_at as Date).getMonth();       const predictableMonths = [8, 9, 10];       const isPredictable = predictableMonths.includes(month) && /(rentre\|scolaire\|saison\|prevu)/i.test(t.title);       let strength = 0.55;       if (isHighValue) strength += 0.10;       const cohort = await ctx.db.bids.findCommonLosers({ winners: [lowest.bidder], minCoincidences: 3, windowDays: 180 });       if (cohort.length > 0) strength += 0.10;       strength = Math.min(0.9, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-A-006',         tenderRef: t.ref,         strength,         evidence: {           procuring_entity: t.procuring_entity,           bid_count: bids.length,           lowest_amount: lowest.amount,           median_amount: median.amount,           spread_pct: spread * 100,           winner: lowest.bidder,           repeated_losing_cohort: cohort         },         evidenceCids: [t.documentCid].filter(Boolean) as string[],         modifiers: {           cluster_at_top_with_outlier_winner: winnerIsOutlierLow,           common_bidder_across_tenders: cohort.length > 0,           spread_within_2pct: tightCluster,           genuine_competitive_spread_pattern: false         },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract'; import { runCypher } from '@vigil/graph-queries';   export const pF001RoundTripPayment: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-F-001',   category: 'F',   display_name_fr: 'Schema de paiement circulaire',   display_name_en: 'Round-trip payment scheme',   severity_baseline: 0.7,   inputs: [{ name: 'payment_orders', source: 'event:document.captured(minfi)', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.008,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.40,     modifiers: [       { when: 'cycle_closes_within_30_days', delta: +0.15 },       { when: 'cycle_amount_within_5pct', delta: +0.18 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const cypher = `       MATCH path = (a:Entity)-[r1:PAID_TO]->(b:Entity)-[r2:PAID_TO]->(c:Entity)-[r3:PAID_TO]->(a)       WHERE r1.amount IS NOT NULL AND r2.amount IS NOT NULL AND r3.amount IS NOT NULL         AND r3.date >= r1.date AND r3.date - r1.date <= duration('P30D')         AND abs(r1.amount - r3.amount) / r1.amount < 0.05       RETURN a.canonical_name AS entityA, b.canonical_name AS entityB, c.canonical_name AS entityC,              r1.amount AS amount, r1.date AS startDate, r3.date AS endDate       LIMIT 200     `;     const cycles = await runCypher(ctx.graph, cypher);     for (const cyc of cycles) {       const days = (cyc.endDate.getTime() - cyc.startDate.getTime()) / 86400_000;       const tightCycle = days <= 30;       let strength = 0.55;       if (tightCycle) strength += 0.15;       strength = Math.min(0.9, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-F-001',         strength,         evidence: {           cycle: [cyc.entityA, cyc.entityB, cyc.entityC, cyc.entityA],           amount: cyc.amount,           start_date: cyc.startDate,           end_date: cyc.endDate,           days: days         },         evidenceCids: [],         modifiers: { cycle_closes_within_30_days: tightCycle, cycle_amount_within_5pct: true },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

    }     return matches;   } }; |

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract'; import { compareSignatures } from '@vigil/forensics';   export const pG002SignatureMismatch: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-G-002',   category: 'G',   display_name_fr: 'Signature incompatible avec le signataire declare',   display_name_en: 'Signature mismatch with declared signatory',   severity_baseline: 0.65,   inputs: [{ name: 'document', source: 'event:document.captured', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.005,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.35,     modifiers: [       { when: 'similarity_below_0_60', delta: +0.18 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const docs = await ctx.db.documents.findRecentSigned({ since: ctx.window.since });     for (const d of docs) {       if (!d.declared_signatory_id) continue;       const declaredSamples = await ctx.db.signatureSamples.findByPersonId(d.declared_signatory_id);       if (declaredSamples.length === 0) continue;       const cmp = await compareSignatures({ documentCid: d.cid, samples: declaredSamples });       if (cmp.maxSimilarity > 0.65) continue;       let strength = 0.6;       if (cmp.maxSimilarity < 0.45) strength += 0.10;       strength = Math.min(0.85, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-G-002',         strength,         evidence: {           documentCid: d.cid,           declared_signatory_id: d.declared_signatory_id,           declared_signatory_name: d.declared_signatory_name,           signature_similarity_max: cmp.maxSimilarity,           samples_compared: declaredSamples.length         },         evidenceCids: [d.cid],         modifiers: { similarity_below_0_60: cmp.maxSimilarity < 0.60 },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract'; import { extractPdfMetadata, extractDocxMetadata } from '@vigil/forensics';   export const pG003MetadataAnomaly: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-G-003',   category: 'G',   display_name_fr: 'Anomalie de metadonnees',   display_name_en: 'Metadata anomaly',   severity_baseline: 0.5,   inputs: [{ name: 'document', source: 'event:document.captured', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.012,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.18,     modifiers: [       { when: 'producer_inconsistent_with_authority', delta: +0.18 },       { when: 'last_modified_post_publication_by_authority', delta: +0.10 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const docs = await ctx.db.documents.findRecentNotYetForensicallyChecked({ since: ctx.window.since });     for (const d of docs) {       const meta = d.mime_type === 'application/pdf' ? | import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract'; import { extractFontList } from '@vigil/forensics';   export const pG004FontAnomaly: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-G-004',   category: 'G',   display_name_fr: 'Anomalie typographique dans document officiel',   display_name_en: 'Font/typography anomaly in official document',   severity_baseline: 0.45,   inputs: [{ name: 'document', source: 'event:document.captured', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.008,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.20,     modifiers: [       { when: 'embedded_font_replaced_inline', delta: +0.18 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const docs = await ctx.db.documents.findRecentOfficial({ since: ctx.window.since });     for (const d of docs) {       const fonts = await extractFontList(d.cid, ctx);       // Heuristic: official Cameroon publications standardise on Times-Roman or Calibri. | import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract';   export const pH001AwardBeforeTenderClose: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-H-001',   category: 'H',   display_name_fr: 'Attribution avant cloture de l\'appel d\'offres',   display_name_en: 'Award issued before tender close date',   severity_baseline: 0.85,   inputs: [{ name: 'award', source: 'event:award.issued', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.004,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.65,     modifiers: [       { when: 'awarded_more_than_3_days_before_close', delta: +0.20 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const awards = await ctx.db.awards.findRecent({ since: ctx.window.since });     for (const a of awards) {       const tender = await ctx.db.tenders.findByRef(a.tender_ref);       if (!tender \|\| !tender.closing_date) continue;       const gap = (tender.closing_date.getTime() - a.award_date.getTime()) / 86400_000;       if (gap <= 0) continue;       let strength = 0.85;       if (gap >= 3) strength += 0.10;       strength = Math.min(0.97, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-H-001',         awardRef: a.ref,         strength,         evidence: {           tender_ref: a.tender_ref,           tender_closing_date: tender.closing_date,           award_date: a.award_date,           gap_days: gap         },         evidenceCids: [a.documentCid, tender.documentCid].filter(Boolean) as string[],         modifiers: { awarded_more_than_3_days_before_close: gap >= 3 },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract';   export const pH002AmendmentOutOfSequence: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-H-002',   category: 'H',   display_name_fr: 'Avenant emis hors sequence',   display_name_en: 'Amendment filed out of sequence',   severity_baseline: 0.55,   inputs: [{ name: 'amendment', source: 'event:amendment.filed', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.012,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.25,     modifiers: [       { when: 'amendment_dated_before_amendment_subject_event', delta: +0.18 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const amendments = await ctx.db.amendments.findRecent({ since: ctx.window.since });     for (const a of amendments) {       const baseAward = await ctx.db.awards.findByRef(a.contract_ref);       if (!baseAward) continue;       // Anomaly: amendment dated earlier than the award's official approval       if (a.dated_at >= baseAward.award_date) continue;       const gap = (baseAward.award_date.getTime() - a.dated_at.getTime()) / 86400_000;       let strength = 0.55;       if (gap >= 30) strength += 0.10;       strength = Math.min(0.88, strength);       matches.push({         patternId: 'P-H-002',         awardRef: baseAward.ref,         strength,         evidence: {           contract_ref: a.contract_ref,           base_award_date: baseAward.award_date,           amendment_dated_at: a.dated_at,           gap_days_amendment_before_award: gap         },         evidenceCids: [a.documentCid, baseAward.documentCid].filter(Boolean) as string[],         modifiers: { amendment_dated_before_amendment_subject_event: true },         detectedAt: new Date()       });     }     return matches;   } }; |

| import type { PatternDef, DetectContext, PatternMatch } from '../contract';   const HOLIDAY_WINDOWS = [   { name: 'Christmas-NYE', start: '12-22', end: '01-03' },   { name: 'Easter', start: '04-04', end: '04-12' },   { name: 'August', start: '08-08', end: '08-22' },   { name: 'Labor Day', start: '04-30', end: '05-03' } ];   function inHolidayWindow(d: Date): string \| null {   const md = `${String(d.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')}-${String(d.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')}`;   for (const w of HOLIDAY_WINDOWS) {     if (w.start <= md && md <= w.end) return w.name;     if (w.start > w.end && (md >= w.start \|\| md <= w.end)) return w.name;   }   return null; }   export const pH003HolidayPublicationBurst: PatternDef = {   id: 'P-H-003',   category: 'H',   display_name_fr: 'Pic de publications pendant les jours feries',   display_name_en: 'Burst of publications during holiday window',   severity_baseline: 0.5,   inputs: [{ name: 'tender', source: 'event:tender.published', required: true }],   expected_hit_rate: 0.018,   bayesian_priors: {     base: 0.18,     modifiers: [       { when: 'burst_above_3x_baseline', delta: +0.15 },       { when: 'closing_date_within_holiday_window', delta: +0.20 }     ]   },     async detect(ctx: DetectContext): Promise<PatternMatch[]> {     const matches: PatternMatch[] = [];     const recent = await ctx.db.tenders.findRecent({ since: ctx.window.since });     const inHoliday = recent.filter((t) => inHolidayWindow(t.published_at));     if (inHoliday.length < 3) return matches;     const baseline = await ctx.db.tenders.dailyAverage({ rollingDays: 90 });     const observedRate = inHoliday.length / 7; // approximate daily rate during holiday week     const ratio = observedRate / baseline;     if (ratio < 2) return matches;     let strength = 0.5;     if (ratio >= 3) strength += 0.10;     if (inHoliday.some((t) => t.closing_date && inHolidayWindow(t.closing_date))) strength += 0.10;     strength = Math.min(0.82, strength);     matches.push({       patternId: 'P-H-003',       strength,       evidence: {         publications_in_window: inHoliday.length,         baseline_daily: baseline,         observed_daily: observedRate,         ratio,         sample_tenders: inHoliday.slice(0, 10).map((t) => ({ ref: t.ref, published_at: t.published_at, closing_date: t.closing_date }))       },       evidenceCids: inHoliday.slice(0, 10).map((t) => t.documentCid).filter(Boolean) as string[],       modifiers: {         burst_above_3x_baseline: ratio >= 3,         closing_date_within_holiday_window: inHoliday.some((t) => t.closing_date && inHolidayWindow(t.closing_date))       },       detectedAt: new Date()     });     return matches;   } }; |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Inject, Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { DocumentService } from './services/document.service'; import { OcrService } from './services/ocr.service'; import { call } from '@vigil/llm-router'; import { documentClassifyPrompt } from '@vigil/prompts'; import { detectLanguage } from '@vigil/lang';   @Processor('document_ocr') export class DocumentProcessor {   private readonly logger = new Logger(DocumentProcessor.name);     constructor(     private readonly docs: DocumentService,     private readonly ocr: OcrService,   ) {}     @Process({ name: 'process-document', concurrency: 4 })   async handle(job: Job<{ documentCid: string; runId: string; sourceMimeType: string }>) {     const { documentCid, runId, sourceMimeType } = job.data;     const t0 = Date.now();     const bytes = await this.docs.fetchByCid(documentCid);     const text = sourceMimeType === 'application/pdf'       ? await this.ocr.extractFromPdf(bytes)       : await this.ocr.extractFromImage(bytes);     if (!text \|\| text.length < 20) {       this.logger.warn({ documentCid }, 'document.ocr.empty-text');       return { skipped: true, reason: 'empty_text' };     }     const language = detectLanguage(text);     const classifyResp = await call({       tier: 'haiku',       systemPrompt: documentClassifyPrompt.system,       userPrompt: documentClassifyPrompt.user(text.slice(0, 4000)),       maxTokens: 200,       temperature: 0,       callerWorker: 'worker-document'     });     const out = classifyResp.output as { document_type: string; confidence: number };     await this.docs.persistEnriched({       cid: documentCid,       text,       language,       document_type: out.document_type,       classifier_confidence: out.confidence,       ocr_duration_ms: Date.now() - t0,       runId     });     return { documentCid, document_type: out.document_type, language, latency_ms: Date.now() - t0 };   } } |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Inject, Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { FindingService } from './services/finding.service';     constructor(private readonly findings: FindingService) {}     @Process({ name: 'extract-evidence', concurrency: 4 })   async handle(job: Job<{     patternId: string;     matchEvidence: Record<string, unknown>;     contextDocs: { cid: string; text: string }[];     runId: string;     tenderRef?: string;     awardRef?: string;   }>) {     const { patternId, matchEvidence, contextDocs, runId } = job.data;     const pattern = patternById.get(patternId);     if (!pattern) throw new Error(`unknown pattern: ${patternId}`);     const resp = await call({       tier: 'sonnet',       systemPrompt: patternEvidencePrompt.system,       userPrompt: patternEvidencePrompt.user({         pattern_id: patternId,         pattern_display_fr: pattern.display_name_fr,         pattern_display_en: pattern.display_name_en,         deterministic_match_evidence: matchEvidence,         context_documents: contextDocs.map((d) => ({ cid: d.cid, excerpt: d.text.slice(0, 6000) }))       }),       maxTokens: 1500,       temperature: 0,       callerWorker: 'worker-extract'     });       uncertainty_factors: string[];       llm_strength_estimate: number;     };     const ref = await this.findings.createDraft({       patternId,       runId,       tenderRef: job.data.tenderRef,       awardRef: job.data.awardRef,       summary: draft.finding_summary,       evidence_items: draft.evidence_items,       counter_evidence_considered: draft.counter_evidence_considered,       uncertainty_factors: draft.uncertainty_factors,       llm_strength_estimate: draft.llm_strength_estimate,       llm_model: resp.model,       llm_input_tokens: resp.input_tokens,       llm_output_tokens: resp.output_tokens     });     return { findingRef: ref };   } } |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { BayesianService } from './services/bayesian.service'; import { FindingService } from './services/finding.service';   @Processor('finding_aggregation') export class BayesianProcessor {   private readonly logger = new Logger(BayesianProcessor.name);     constructor(     private readonly bayes: BayesianService,     private readonly findings: FindingService   ) {}     @Process({ name: 'recompute-aggregate', concurrency: 2 })   async handle(job: Job<{ entityId: string; runId: string }>) {     const { entityId, runId } = job.data;     const findings = await this.findings.findByEntityId(entityId);     if (findings.length < 2) return { skipped: true, reason: 'fewer_than_two_findings' };       // Combine independent findings via log-odds addition with diminishing-returns cap     let logOdds = 0;     const independentEvidenceSources = new Set<string>();     for (const f of findings) {       const sourceKey = f.principal_evidence_source;       if (independentEvidenceSources.has(sourceKey)) continue;       independentEvidenceSources.add(sourceKey);       const odds = f.posterior / (1 - f.posterior);       logOdds += Math.log(odds);     }     let aggregated = Math.exp(logOdds) / (1 + Math.exp(logOdds));     aggregated = Math.min(0.99, aggregated);       await this.bayes.persistEntityRiskScore({       entityId,       score: aggregated,       contributing_finding_refs: findings.map((f) => f.ref),       independent_source_count: independentEvidenceSources.size,       runId     });     return { entityId, aggregated, contributingFindings: findings.length };   } } |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { FindingService } from './services/finding.service'; import { call } from '@vigil/llm-router'; import { devilsAdvocatePrompt } from '@vigil/prompts';   @Processor('counter_evidence') export class CounterEvidenceProcessor {   private readonly logger = new Logger(CounterEvidenceProcessor.name);     constructor(private readonly findings: FindingService) {}     @Process({ name: 'rebut-finding', concurrency: 2 })   async handle(job: Job<{ findingRef: string; runId: string }>) {     const { findingRef, runId } = job.data;     const finding = await this.findings.getByRef(findingRef);     if (!finding) throw new Error('finding-not-found: ' + findingRef);     const tier = finding.posterior >= 0.92 ? 'opus' : 'sonnet';     const resp = await call({       tier,       systemPrompt: devilsAdvocatePrompt.system,       userPrompt: devilsAdvocatePrompt.user({         finding_summary: finding.summary,         evidence_items: finding.evidence_items,         posterior: finding.posterior,         pattern_id: finding.pattern_id       }),       maxTokens: 2000,       temperature: 0,       callerWorker: 'worker-counter-evidence'     });     const out = resp.output as {       rebuttals_identified: Array<{ rebuttal: string; weight: 'STRONG'\|'MODERATE'\|'WEAK'; source_basis: string }>;       no_rebuttal_identified: boolean;       reweighting_recommendation: { adjust_strength_by: number };     };     await this.findings.attachCounterEvidence({       findingRef,       rebuttals: out.rebuttals_identified,       no_rebuttal_identified: out.no_rebuttal_identified,       reweighting: out.reweighting_recommendation,       llm_model: resp.model,       runId     });     if (out.reweighting_recommendation && out.reweighting_recommendation.adjust_strength_by !== 0) {       await this.findings.adjustPosterior({         findingRef,         delta: out.reweighting_recommendation.adjust_strength_by,         reason: 'counter_evidence_reweighting',         runId       });     }     return { findingRef, hadRebuttal: !out.no_rebuttal_identified, rebuttalCount: out.rebuttals_identified.length };   } } |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { FindingService } from './services/finding.service'; import { DossierRenderer } from './services/dossier-renderer.service'; import { AnchorService } from './services/anchor.service'; import { call } from '@vigil/llm-router'; import { dossierTranslatePrompt, councilSummaryPrompt } from '@vigil/prompts';   @Processor('dossier_render') export class DossierProcessor {   private readonly logger = new Logger(DossierProcessor.name);     constructor(     private readonly findings: FindingService,     private readonly renderer: DossierRenderer,     private readonly anchor: AnchorService   ) {}     @Process({ name: 'render-dossier', concurrency: 1 })   async handle(job: Job<{ findingRef: string; runId: string }>) {     const { findingRef, runId } = job.data;     const finding = await this.findings.getByRef(findingRef);     if (!finding) throw new Error('finding-not-found');       const summaryResp = await call({       tier: 'opus',       systemPrompt: councilSummaryPrompt.system,       userPrompt: councilSummaryPrompt.user({ finding }),       maxTokens: 2500,       temperature: 0,       callerWorker: 'worker-dossier'     });     const fr_summary = (summaryResp.output as any).summary_fr;     const en_translation = await call({       tier: 'sonnet',       systemPrompt: dossierTranslatePrompt.system,       userPrompt: dossierTranslatePrompt.user({ source_text: fr_summary, source_language: 'fr', target_language: 'en' }),       maxTokens: 2500,       temperature: 0,       callerWorker: 'worker-dossier'     });     const en_summary = (en_translation.output as any).translation;       const dossierBuffer = await this.renderer.render({       finding,       fr_summary,       en_summary,       evidence_items: finding.evidence_items,       counter_evidence: finding.counter_evidence,       methodology_appendix: this.renderer.standardMethodologyAppendix()     });     const dossierCid = await this.findings.persistDossier({ findingRef, dossierBuffer });     const anchorTx = await this.anchor.commit({       finding_ref: finding.ref,       dossier_cid: dossierCid,       posterior: finding.posterior,       summary_hash: dossierBuffer.summaryHash     });     await this.findings.recordAnchor({ findingRef, dossierCid, anchorTx, runId });     return { findingRef, dossierCid, anchorTx };   } } |

| import { Process, Processor } from '@nestjs/bullmq'; import { Logger } from '@nestjs/common'; import type { Job } from 'bullmq'; import { FindingService } from './services/finding.service'; import { SftpClient } from './services/sftp-client.service'; import { GpgService } from './services/gpg.service'; import { AnchorService } from './services/anchor.service'; import * as path from 'path';   @Processor('conac_delivery') export class ConacSftpProcessor {   private readonly logger = new Logger(ConacSftpProcessor.name);     constructor(     private readonly findings: FindingService,     private readonly sftp: SftpClient,     private readonly gpg: GpgService,     private readonly anchor: AnchorService   ) {}     @Process({ name: 'deliver-to-conac', concurrency: 1 })   async handle(job: Job<{ findingRef: string; runId: string }>) {     const { findingRef, runId } = job.data;     const finding = await this.findings.getByRef(findingRef);     if (!finding) throw new Error('finding-not-found');     if (!finding.dossier_cid) throw new Error('dossier-not-rendered');       const dossierBytes = await this.findings.fetchDossierBytes(finding.dossier_cid);     const encrypted = await this.gpg.encryptForRecipients(dossierBytes, ['conac-vigil@conac.cm']);     const remoteName = `vigil-${finding.ref}-${Date.now()}.pdf.gpg`;     await this.sftp.upload({ remotePath: `/inbox/${remoteName}`, buffer: encrypted });     await this.findings.recordDelivery({ findingRef, channel: 'conac-sftp', remotePath: `/inbox/${remoteName}`, status: 'UPLOADED', runId });       // Poll for ACK file at /ack/<ref>.ack with 60s timeout     const ackName = `/ack/${finding.ref}.ack`;     const deadline = Date.now() + 60_000;     let ackText: string \| null = null;     while (Date.now() < deadline) {       ackText = await this.sftp.tryFetch(ackName).catch(() => null);       if (ackText) break;       await new Promise((r) => setTimeout(r, 5000));     }     if (!ackText) {       this.logger.warn({ findingRef }, 'conac.ack-timeout');       await this.findings.recordDelivery({ findingRef, channel: 'conac-sftp', remotePath: `/inbox/${remoteName}`, status: 'AWAITING_ACK', runId });       return { findingRef, status: 'AWAITING_ACK' };     }     await this.findings.recordDelivery({ findingRef, channel: 'conac-sftp', remotePath: `/inbox/${remoteName}`, status: 'ACKNOWLEDGED', ack: ackText, runId });     const anchorTx = await this.anchor.commit({ finding_ref: finding.ref, delivery_channel: 'conac-sftp', ack_hash: this.gpg.hash(ackText) });     return { findingRef, status: 'ACKNOWLEDGED', anchorTx };   } } |
